0.4).astype('uint8')\n        if random.random() > 0.96:\n            frame = (frame * 0.7 + np.random.randint(0, 80, frame.shape, dtype='uint8')).astype('uint8')\n        if random.random() > 0.99:\n            frame = 255 - frame\n        return frame\n    \n    final_video = final_video.fl(apply_global_glitch)\n    output_path = os.path.join(BASE_PATH, OUTPUT_NAME)\n "1455_1|U||G|REPO|prism-audio-flux-engine|ACTIVE_RESEARCH|1|в”ңв”Җв”Җ LICENSE\\nв”ңв”Җв”Җ README.md\\nв”ңв”Җв”Җ prism_engine.sh\\n<span style='color:#8b949e; font-size:0.9em;'>0 directories, 3 files</span>|NULL|MIT|# рҹҢҢ PRISM AUDIO FLUX ENGINE\nAutomated bash script for algorithmic audio mutation and re-synthesis. Not a standard remix tool; refracts audio into unpredictable textures. Optimized for 24-bit/96kHz FLAC (UAPP/Hi-Res).\n> \"Music is frequency arranged in time. If the arrangement is stagnant, reality is stagnant. We mutate it.\" вҖ” Chimera Core\n---\n## вңЁ Key Features\n* **Zero-Loss Ingestion**: Supports filenames with spaces, Japanese/Chinese characters, and symbols via null-terminated processing.\n* **Universal Decoding**: Processes MP3, FLAC, WAV, M4A, OPUS, MP4 into 32-bit float format.\n* **Independent Logic**: Randomizes time stretch (0.88x-1.12x) and pitch (-400 to +200 cents) separately.\n* **Mastering**: Anti-clipping gain staging (-3dB) and soft-knee limiter.\n* **High-Res**: Upsamples to 96kHz to eliminate aliasing during pitch shifting.\n---\n## рҹ”® Mutation Modes\n1. **Neon Piano**: Metallic resonance, phaser feedback, highpass filter.\n2. **Liquid Silk**: Warm analog tape vibe, lowpass 4500Hz, overdrive.\n3. **Deep Future**: Heavy bass boost, compressed dynamics, submerged vocals.\n4. **Cyber Jazz**: Mid-range clarity, high contrast, punchy EQ.\n5. **Vapor Tape**: Sinc filtering, lo-fi degradation, saturation.\n---\n## рҹӣ пёҸ Usage\n### Prerequisites\n* **OS**: Linux or Android (Termux).\n* **Packages**: `sox`, `ffmpeg`, `libsox-fmt-all`.\n### 1. Setup\n```bash\npkg update && pkg upgrade\npkg install sox ffmpeg git -y\n```\n### 2. Install\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/ChimeraCoreLab/prism-audio-flux-engine.git\ncd prism-audio-flux-engine\nchmod +x prism_engine.sh\n```\n### 3. Run\nEdit `SOURCE_DIR` in `prism_engine.sh`, then execute:\n```bash\n./prism_engine.sh\n```\n*Variants saved in `PRISM_VARIANTS` subfolder.*\n---\n## вҡ–пёҸ License\nMIT License.
